<div dir="auto"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto" class="heading-element">Scroll &amp; zoom</h2><a id="user-content-scroll--zoom" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Scroll &amp; zoom" href="#scroll--zoom"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div><a id="user-content-scroll--zoom" aria-label="Permalink: Scroll &amp; zoom" href="#scroll--zoom"></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Mousewheel</strong> | <strong>2 fingers horizontal</strong> (Trackpad): vertical scroll</li>
<li><strong>Shift + Mousewheel</strong> | <strong>2 fingers vertical</strong> (Trackpad): horizontal scroll</li>
<li><strong>Alt + Mousewheel</strong> | <strong>Alt + 2 fingers</strong>: horizontal zoom</li>
<li><strong>Alt + Mousewheel</strong> | <strong>Alt + 2 fingers</strong> - left columun: vertical zoom</li>
<li><strong>z</strong> (without selection): horizontal zoom to display all moments</li>
<li><strong>z</strong> (with selection): horizontal zoom on selected moments</li>
<li><strong>n</strong>: scroll to the current date and time</li>
</ul>
<div dir="auto"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto" class="heading-element">Selection</h2><a id="user-content-selection" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Selection" href="#selection"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div><a id="user-content-selection" aria-label="Permalink: Selection" href="#selection"></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Shift + click</strong> on existing moments: multi-selection</li>
<li><strong>Click &amp; drag</strong>: multi-selection lasso</li>
<li><strong>Shift + click &amp; drag</strong> : add to the current selection</li>
<li><strong>Click sur nom de ligne</strong> : selection of the whole line</li>
</ul>
<div dir="auto"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto" class="heading-element">Creation / modification</h2><a id="user-content-creation--modification" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Creation / modification" href="#creation--modification"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div><a id="user-content-creation--modification" aria-label="Permalink: Creation / modification" href="#creation--modification"></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Alt + Click &amp; drag</strong>: moment creation</li>
<li><strong>Alt + Click &amp; drag</strong> on an existing moment: duplicate a moment at another date</li>
<li><strong>d</strong>: duplicate selected moments</li>
<li><strong>s</strong>: split the selected moments at the position of the blue cursor</li>
</ul>
